 We have suggestions for sustainable makeup in humid weather
 * agar aapke chehre par zyada daag-dhabbe or halke gaddhe yaa dane hai, tabhi mechap-primer lagaaein kyonki aisa karnaa is mausam main upyukt hoga, yah twachaa kii sataha ko samtal kar degaa or isse mechap zyada der tak tikaa rahegaa, lekin jinhen aisi samasya nahin hai, unhen primer lagane kii koi jarurat nahin he
 * a mild coat of oil-free moisturizer may be applied instead of a liquid or cream foundation due to the possibility of sweating with sweat during humid weather, applying a lightweight compact powder for touch-up
 * agar aap daag-dhabbon yaa kaale ghare ko chhipaana chaahati hai to oil-free concillar laga sakati hai, kyonki oil yukt concillar umas main chehre ko chipchipa or taileey banaata he
 Always choose only oil-free makeup products
 * monsoon ke dauraan hameshaa is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen ki aapkaa blash saumy or paridhaan ko suut karte hue hona chahie
 Buy powdered eyeshadow as these creams last longer than eye shadows
 halkaa rang kaa thodaa sa ai shadow lagaaein
 * Apply liquid eyeliner as these are more durable than waxed eyeliner pencils
 tippaniyan * Apply waterproof mascara on eyelashes, it will last longer

 It is not appropriate to apply lip balm in this season
 input ieenes se * If you have more spots and mild pits or pimples on your face, then only apply makeup-primer as it will be suitable in this season, it will flatten the surface of the skin and this will make the makeup last longer, but such There are no problems, there is no need to apply primer
